</font><font color="#800000">A rhythmic thrumming saturates the area, drawing attention to a war shrine of
 Terentia nearby.</font><font color="#008080"> Shimmering liquid coruscates throughout the bluish archway,
 refracting all available light and casting a wavering ambiance over the area.
